country_event = { #Army of the Dead 2 - The Acquisition of Bodies
	id = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.3
	title = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.3.t
	desc = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.3.d
	picture = muslimgfx_PLAGUE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event }
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.4 } }
		}
		else = {
			clr_country_flag = aotd_1M
			clr_country_flag = aotd_100k
			clr_country_flag = aotd_10k
			clr_country_flag = aotd_1k
			clr_country_flag = aotd_100
			clr_country_flag = aotd_10
		}
	}

	option = { #More bodies!
		name = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.3.a

		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = aotd_1M }
			if = {
				limit = { manpower = 1000 }
				add_manpower = -1000
				increase_magic_experience = { amount = 10 }
				add_ae_for_known_countries_with_limit = { value = 5 limit = "NOT = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = army_of_the_dead level = 1 } }" desc = not_unlocked_aotd_tt }
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = aotd_not_enough_manpower_tt
				clr_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = aotd_100k }
			if = {
				limit = { manpower = 100 }
				add_manpower = -100
				increase_magic_experience = { amount = 10 }
				add_ae_for_known_countries_with_limit = { value = 5 limit = "NOT = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = army_of_the_dead level = 1 } }" desc = not_unlocked_aotd_tt }
				clr_country_flag = aotd_100k
				set_country_flag = aotd_1M
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = aotd_not_enough_manpower_tt
				clr_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = aotd_10k }
			if = {
				limit = { manpower = 10 }
				add_manpower = -10
				increase_magic_experience = { amount = 10 }
				add_ae_for_known_countries_with_limit = { value = 5 limit = "NOT = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = army_of_the_dead level = 1 } }" desc = not_unlocked_aotd_tt }
				clr_country_flag = aotd_10k
				set_country_flag = aotd_100k
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = aotd_not_enough_manpower_tt
				clr_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = aotd_1k }
			if = {
				limit = { manpower = 1 }
				add_manpower = -1
				increase_magic_experience = { amount = 10 }
				add_ae_for_known_countries_with_limit = { value = 5 limit = "NOT = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = army_of_the_dead level = 1 } }" desc = not_unlocked_aotd_tt }
				clr_country_flag = aotd_1k
				set_country_flag = aotd_10k
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = aotd_not_enough_manpower_tt
				clr_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = aotd_100 }
			if = {
				limit = { manpower = 0.1 }
				add_manpower = -0.1
				increase_magic_experience = { amount = 10 }
				add_ae_for_known_countries_with_limit = { value = 5 limit = "NOT = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = army_of_the_dead level = 1 } }" desc = not_unlocked_aotd_tt }
				clr_country_flag = aotd_100
				set_country_flag = aotd_1k
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = aotd_not_enough_manpower_tt
				clr_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = aotd_10 }
			if = {
				limit = { manpower = 0.01 }
				add_manpower = -0.01
				increase_magic_experience = { amount = 5 }
				add_ae_for_known_countries_with_limit = { value = 2 limit = "NOT = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = army_of_the_dead level = 1 } }" desc = not_unlocked_aotd_tt }
				clr_country_flag = aotd_10
				set_country_flag = aotd_100
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = aotd_not_enough_manpower_tt
				clr_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = {
				limit = { manpower = 0.001 }
				add_manpower = -0.001
				increase_magic_experience = { amount = 1 }
				add_ae_for_known_countries_with_limit = { value = 1 limit = "NOT = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = army_of_the_dead level = 1 } }" desc = not_unlocked_aotd_tt }
				set_country_flag = aotd_10
			}
			else = {
				custom_tooltip = aotd_not_enough_manpower_tt
				clr_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #That's enough bodies
		name = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.3.b
		clr_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event
	}
}

country_event = { #Undead Army gains manpower on winning battles
	id = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.20
	title = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.20.t
	desc = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.20.d
	picture = UNDEAD_ARMY_eventPicture
	
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	trigger = { check_variable = { raise_undead = 3001 } } #Don't raise if it was a nothing battle
	
	option = {	#Rise!
		name = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.20.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

		divide_variable = { raise_undead = 3 } #33% of the dead are raised
		round_variable = { #truncate decimal portion
			which = raise_undead
			value = -1
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = hide_necromancy_on_battle }
			divide_variable = { raise_undead = 1000 }
			var_effect_granular = { effect = add_manpower var = raise_undead sign = + }
		}
		else = {
			country_event = { id = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.21 }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Undead Army Manpower notif event
	id = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.21
	title = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.21.t
	desc = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.21.d
	picture = UNDEAD_ARMY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			divide_variable = { raise_undead = 1000 }
			var_effect_granular = { effect = add_manpower var = raise_undead sign = + }
		}
	}

	option = {	#Rise!
		name = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.21.a
		
		custom_tooltip = magic_spell_raise_undead_tt
	}
	
	option = {	#Rise! (But hide these pop-ups from now on)
		name = magic_project_army_of_the_dead.21.b
		
		custom_tooltip = magic_spell_raise_undead_tt
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = hide_necromancy_on_battle }
	}
}

##################
### HOMUNCULUS ###
##################
#1 - Make the core
#2 - Make the body
#3 - Bind it to you
#4 - Decide what to do with it
#5 - (If applicable) Decide whether to stay quiet or go loud

namespace = magic_project_homunculus

country_event = { #Homunculus event handler
	id = magic_project_homunculus.0
	title = magic_project_homunculus.0.t
	desc = magic_project_homunculus.0.d
	picture = ANGRY_MOB_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = magic_project_completed_flag }
			if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 3 } }
				country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.7 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 2 } }
				country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.6 }
			}
			else = { country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.5 } }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 33 }
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = studying_homunculus_body_mud
					has_country_modifier = studying_homunculus_body_stone
					has_country_modifier = studying_homunculus_body_blood
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.3 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 67 }
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = studying_homunculus_loyalty_law
					has_country_modifier = studying_homunculus_loyalty_child
					has_country_modifier = studying_homunculus_loyalty_magic
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.4 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = magic_project_homunculus.0.a
	}
}

country_event = { #Homunculus bounceback for trying old options
	id = magic_project_homunculus.1
	title = magic_project_homunculus.1.t
	desc = magic_project_homunculus.1.d
	picture = CIVIL_WAR_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = magic_project_homunculus.1.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_country_flag

			homunculus_in_event_1 = { clr_country_flag = homunculus_in_event_1 country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.2 } }
			homunculus_in_event_2 = { clr_country_flag = homunculus_in_event_2 country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.3 } }
			homunculus_in_event_3 = { clr_country_flag = homunculus_in_event_3 country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.4 } }
			homunculus_in_event_4 = { clr_country_flag = homunculus_in_event_4 country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.8 } }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Homunculus 1 - Heart
	id = magic_project_homunculus.2
	title = magic_project_homunculus.2.t
	desc = magic_project_homunculus.2.d
	picture = INVENTION_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { set_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event }

	after = {
		clr_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = homunculus_in_event_1 }
				country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Animal Heart
		name = magic_project_homunculus.2.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = homunculus_tried_option_1_1 } }

		if = {
			limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 1 } }
			custom_tooltip = homunculus_already_tried
			set_country_flag = homunculus_in_event_1
			set_country_flag = homunculus_tried_option_1_1
			tooltip = {
				random_owned_province = { add_devastation = 1 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = studying_homunculus_core_animal duration = -1 desc = until_advancement_concludes }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_owned_province = { add_devastation = 1 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = studying_homunculus_core_animal duration = -1 desc = until_advancement_concludes }
		}
	}
	
	option = {	#Clockwork Mechanism
		name = magic_project_homunculus.2.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			at_least_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 1 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = homunculus_tried_option_1_2 }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 2 } }
			custom_tooltip = homunculus_already_tried
			set_country_flag = homunculus_in_event_1
			set_country_flag = homunculus_tried_option_1_2
			tooltip = {
				add_treasury = -120
				add_country_modifier = { name = studying_homunculus_core_clockwork duration = -1 desc = until_advancement_concludes }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_treasury = -120
			add_country_modifier = { name = studying_homunculus_core_clockwork duration = -1 desc = until_advancement_concludes }
			clr_country_flag = homunculus_tried_option_1_1
		}
	}
	
	option = {	#A Pure Damestear core
		name = magic_project_homunculus.2.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 2 } }
		
		random_owned_province = {
			add_base_tax = -1
			add_base_production = -1
			add_base_manpower = -1
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = studying_homunculus_core_damestear duration = -1 desc = until_advancement_concludes }

country_event = { #Homunculus 2 - Body
	id = magic_project_homunculus.3
	title = magic_project_homunculus.3.t
	desc = magic_project_homunculus.3.desc
	picture = BUDDHA_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = { set_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event }

	after = {
		clr_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_flag = homunculus_in_event_2 }
				country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {	#Mud Body
		name = magic_project_homunculus.3.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = { NOT = { has_country_flag = homunculus_tried_option_2_1 } }

		if = {
			limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 1 } }
			custom_tooltip = homunculus_already_tried
			set_country_flag = homunculus_in_event_2
			set_country_flag = homunculus_tried_option_2_1
			tooltip = {
				add_prestige = -10
				add_country_modifier = { name = studying_homunculus_body_mud duration = -1 desc = until_advancement_concludes }
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_prestige = -10
			add_country_modifier = { name = studying_homunculus_body_mud duration = -1 desc = until_advancement_concludes }
		}
	}
	
	option = {	#Sculpture Body
		name = magic_project_homunculus.3.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			at_least_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 1 }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = homunculus_tried_option_2_2 }
		}
		
		if = {
			limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 2 } }
			custom_tooltip = homunculus_already_tried
			set_country_flag = homunculus_in_event_2
			set_country_flag = homunculus_tried_option_2_2

				kill_advisor = random
				capital_scope = { add_unrest = 10 }
				add_country_modifier = { name = studying_homunculus_body_stone duration = -1 desc = until_advancement_concludes }
			}
		}
		else = {
			kill_advisor = random
			capital_scope = { add_unrest = 10 }
			add_country_modifier = { name = studying_homunculus_body_stone duration = -1 desc = until_advancement_concludes }
			clr_country_flag = homunculus_tried_option_2_1
		}
	}
	
	option = {	#Concentrated Flesh
		name = magic_project_homunculus.3.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 2 } }

		increase_estate_witch_king_points = { size = large }
		add_manpower = -0.5
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { base_manpower = 2 }
			add_base_manpower = -1
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { base_manpower = 2 }
			add_base_manpower = -1
		}
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = { base_manpower = 2 }
			add_base_manpower = -1
		}
		add_country_modifier = { name = studying_homunculus_body_blood duration = -1 desc = until_advancement_concludes }
		clr_country_flag = homunculus_tried_option_2_1
		clr_country_flag = homunculus_tried_option_2_2
	}

	option = { #No
		name = magic_project_homunculus.3.d
		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_country_flag = homunculus_tried_option_2_1

	}

	option = { #Heir, male
		name = magic_project_homunculus.6.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			has_government_attribute = heir
			NOT = { has_government_attribute = is_magocracy }
			NOT = { has_ruler_flag = xhazob_patron }
			NOT = { has_global_modifier_value = { which = female_advisor_chance value = 1 } }

			male = yes
		}
		set_heir_flag = long_lived_ruler
		set_heir_flag = is_a_homunculus #Keeps them immortal
		set_country_flag = chose_male_homunculus_heir #For repair
		custom_tooltip = homunculus_is_male_tt
		custom_tooltip = tooltip_magic_project_advance
	}
	option = { #Heir, female
		name = magic_project_homunculus.6.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

			NOT = { has_ruler_flag = xhazob_patron }
			has_global_modifier_value = { which = female_advisor_chance value = 0.01 }
			is_lesser_in_union = no
		}
		custom_tooltip = homunculi_no_mage_hint_tt
		remove_heir = {  }
		define_heir = {
			dynasty = ROOT
			age = 20
			adm = 5
			dip = 5
			mil = 5
			claim = 25

		custom_tooltip = homunculus_is_female_tt
		custom_tooltip = tooltip_magic_project_advance
	}
	option = { #Eminince Grise

		show_magic_project_homunculus_warning = yes

	option = { #Mechatriarch
		name = magic_project_homunculus.6.c

			has_government_attribute = queen
			is_lesser_in_union = no
		}

			remove_consort = yes
		}

			limit = { ruler_attracted_to_men = yes }
			define_consort = {
				dynasty = ROOT

				adm = 5
				dip = 5
				mil = 5
				male = yes	
			}
			add_country_modifier = { name = homunculus_consort_m duration = -1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { ruler_attracted_to_women = yes }
			define_consort = {
				dynasty = ROOT
				age = 20
				adm = 5
				dip = 5
				mil = 5
				female = yes
			}
			add_country_modifier = { name = homunculus_consort_f duration = -1 }
		}

		set_consort_flag = long_lived_ruler
		set_consort_flag = is_a_homunculus #Keeps them immortal
		custom_tooltip = tooltip_magic_project_advance
	}

		highlight = yes
		
		add_country_modifier = { name = homunculus_constitutional_custodian duration = -1 }
		custom_tooltip = tooltip_magic_project_advance
	}

country_event = { #Homunculus, Hide or Reveal?
	id = magic_project_homunculus.8
	title = magic_project_homunculus.8.t
	desc = magic_project_homunculus.8.d
	picture = CROSSROAD_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Go loud
		name = magic_project_homunculus.8.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = { exactly_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 2 } }

		add_country_modifier = { name = homunculus_court_unrest duration = 3650 }
		add_dip_power = -100
		anb_add_accepted_culture_or_dip_power = { culture = homunculi free = yes }
	}

	option = { #Stay quiet
		name = magic_project_homunculus.8.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = { NOT = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 3 } } }

		if = {
			limit = { exactly_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 1 } }
			custom_tooltip = homunculus_no_need_tt
			tooltip = {
				country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.15 days = 29200 } #Old Age
				country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.9 days = 3650 random = 32850 } #Discovery!
			}
			set_country_flag = homunculus_in_event_4
			hidden_effect = { country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.1 } }
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = hiding_a_homunculus
			country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.15 days = 29200 } #Old Age
			country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.9 days = 3650 random = 32850 } #Discovery!
		}
	}

	option = { #Too bad, I chose already
		name = magic_project_homunculus.8.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }
		trigger = {
			custom_trigger_tooltip = {
				tooltip = homunculus_no_choose_tt
				at_least_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 3 }
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_country_modifier = { name = homunculus_court_unrest duration = 365 }
	}

	option = { #What are you talking about
		name = magic_project_homunculus.8.e
		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = { exactly_magic_project_level = { project = homunculus level = 1 } }
			if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = homunculus_study }
				has_country_modifier = homunculus_study
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_country_modifier = homunculus_training }
				has_country_modifier = homunculus_training
			}
			else = { has_country_modifier = homunculus_operating_theatre }
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_prestige = -1 #value intended
	}
}

country_event = { #Homunculus reveal event sorter -- these are the worst outcomes
	id = magic_project_homunculus.9
	title = magic_project_homunculus.9.t
	desc = magic_project_homunculus.9.d
	picture = KINGS_CHOICE_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	trigger = { has_country_flag = hiding_a_homunculus }

	option = {
		name = magic_project_homunculus.9.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 1 }

		if = {
			limit = { has_heir_flag = is_a_homunculus }
			country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.10 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_ruler_flag = is_a_homunculus }
			country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.11 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { OR = { has_country_modifier = homunculus_consort_f has_country_modifier = homunculus_consort_m } }
			country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.12 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_modifier = homunculus_eminence_grise
					has_country_modifier = homunculus_constitutional_custodian
					has_country_modifier = homunculus_attendant
				}
			}
			country_event = { id = magic_project_homunculus.13 }
		}
	}
}

	id = magic_project_drennen_project_1.0
	title = magic_project_drennen_project_1.0.t
	desc = magic_project_drennen_project_1.0.d
	picture = SPY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = magic_project_completed_flag }
			country_event = {
				id = magic_project_drennen_project_1.1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 20 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened
			country_event = {
				id = salla_drennen.24
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 40 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened
			country_event = {
				id = salla_drennen.25
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 60 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_third_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_third_event_happened
			country_event = {
				id = salla_drennen.26
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 80 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_fourth_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_fourth_event_happened
			country_event = {
				id = salla_drennen.27
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = magic_project_drennen_project_1.0.a
	}
}

	id = magic_project_umbral_project_spire.10
	title = magic_project_umbral_covenant.10.t
	desc = magic_project_umbral_covenant.10.d

				show_ambient_object = LF_Spire_B_UC_1

					}

				}
				else_if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = { check_variable = { which = S90_secrets_spires_reward value = 3 } }
					}

				else_if = {

country_event = { #HANDLER
	id = magic_project_umbral_project_ashen.0
	title = magic_project_umbral_covenant.50.t
	desc = magic_project_umbral_covenant.50.d
	picture = SPY_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = magic_project_completed_flag }
			country_event = { id = magic_project_umbral_project_ashen.65 } #Divide and conquer
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 12 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened
			country_event = { id = magic_project_umbral_project_ashen.52 } #grounding
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 24 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened
			country_event = { id = magic_project_umbral_project_ashen.53 } #come with me
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 36 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_third_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_third_event_happened
			country_event = { id = magic_project_umbral_project_ashen.54 } #sublimation
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 48 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_fourth_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_fourth_event_happened

		else_if = {

			}
		}
		S70 = {
			remove_country_modifier = S90_by_three
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = S90_komina_I
			duration = -1
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = magic_project_umbral_covenant.65.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
					which = S90_komina_friendship 
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}
		S70 = {
			remove_country_modifier = S90_by_three
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #HANDLER
	id = magic_project_umbral_project_loveme.0
	title = magic_project_umbral_covenant.100.t
	desc = magic_project_umbral_covenant.100.d
	picture = SPY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = magic_project_completed_flag }
			country_event = {
				id = flavor_umbral_covenant.20 #and despair
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 10 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened
			country_event = { id = magic_project_umbral_project_loveme.102 } #Souls for the Spellcraft
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 30 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened
			country_event = { id = magic_project_umbral_project_loveme.103 } #Mana Manipulation
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 50 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_third_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_third_event_happened
			country_event = { id = magic_project_umbral_project_loveme.104 } #Unbind the Beasts
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 70 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_fourth_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_fourth_event_happened
			country_event = { id = magic_project_umbral_project_loveme.105 } #All I Am
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = magic_project_umbral_covenant.100.a
	}
}

### ESTHIL MAGIC PROJECT
namespace = magic_project_esthil_necronomics

# Handler event
country_event = { #Esthil necronomics event handler
	id = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.0
	title = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.0.t
	desc = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.0.d
	picture = END_OF_TIME_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = { #It has to be this complex on account of people stopping and starting research
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = magic_project_completed_flag }
			if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = esthil_necronomics level = 3 } }
				country_event = { id = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.12 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = esthil_necronomics level = 2 } }
				country_event = { id = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.8 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.4 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 33 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened
			if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = esthil_necronomics level = 2 } }
				country_event = { id = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.10 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = esthil_necronomics level = 1 } }
				country_event = { id = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.6 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.2 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 67 }
				NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened }
			}
			set_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened
			if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = esthil_necronomics level = 2 } }
				country_event = { id = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.11 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = esthil_necronomics level = 1 } }
				country_event = { id = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.7 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.3 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.0.a
	}
}

# Prototypes
country_event = {
	id = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.3
	title = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.3.t
	desc = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.3.d
	picture = DEATH_OF_HEIR_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { 
		set_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event 
		hidden_effect = {
			random_owned_province = { limit = { OR = { has_terrain = farmlands has_terrain = grasslands } } 
				save_event_target_as = prov1
				set_province_flag = temp_flag
			}
			random_owned_province = { limit = { OR = { has_terrain = farmlands has_terrain = grasslands } NOT = { has_province_flag = temp_flag } } 
				save_event_target_as = prov2
				set_province_flag = temp_flag
			}
			random_owned_province = { limit = { OR = { has_terrain = farmlands has_terrain = grasslands } NOT = { has_province_flag = temp_flag } } 
				save_event_target_as = prov3
			}
			event_target:prov1 = { clr_province_flag = temp_flag }
			event_target:prov2 = { clr_province_flag = temp_flag }
		}
		
	}
	after = { clr_country_flag = in_magic_progress_event }
	
	option = {
		name = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.3.a
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
	}

	option = {
		name = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.3.b
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = B54_cmod_magic_project_mod_3_1 duration = -1 }
		event_target:prov1 = { spawn_rebels = { size = 1 type = leadered_peasant_rebels } }
	}

	option = {
		name = magic_project_esthil_necronomics.3.c
		ai_chance = { factor = 50 }
		add_country_modifier = { name = B54_cmod_magic_project_mod_3_2 duration = -1 }
		event_target:prov1 = { spawn_rebels = { size = 1 type = leadered_peasant_rebels } }
		event_target:prov2 = { spawn_rebels = { size = 1 type = leadered_peasant_rebels } }
		event_target:prov3 = { spawn_rebels = { size = 1 type = leadered_peasant_rebels } }
	}
}

country_event = { 
	id = magic_project_great_storm_project_1.0
	title = magic_project_great_storm_project_1.0.t
	desc = magic_project_great_storm_project_1.0.d
	picture = SPY_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = magic_project_completed_flag }
			country_event = {
				id = magic_project_great_storm_project_1.1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 25 } NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened } }
			set_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened
			if = { 
				limit = { exactly_magic_project_level = { project = great_storm_project_1 level = 1 } }
				country_event = { id = flavour_great_storm.62 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { exactly_magic_project_level = { project = great_storm_project_1 level = 0 } }
				country_event = { id = flavour_great_storm.52 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 50 } NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened } }
			set_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened
			if = {
				limit = { exactly_magic_project_level = { project = great_storm_project_1 level = 2 } }
				country_event = { id = flavour_great_storm.72 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { exactly_magic_project_level = { project = great_storm_project_1 level = 1 } }
				country_event = { id = flavour_great_storm.63 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	option = {
		name = magic_project_great_storm_project_1.0.a
	}
}

#BLACK HERD PROJECT

namespace = magic_project_black_herd_project_1

country_event = { 
	id = magic_project_black_herd_project_1.0
	title = none
	desc = none
	picture = none

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = magic_project_completed_flag }
			country_event = {
				id = magic_project_black_herd_project_1.1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 50 } NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened } }
			set_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened
			if = { 
				limit = { exactly_magic_project_level = { project = black_herd_project_1 level = 2 } }
				country_event = { id = black_herd_events.31 } #Shattering Stone
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = { exactly_magic_project_level = { project = black_herd_project_1 level = 1 } }
				country_event = { id = black_herd_events.21 } #Spread The Blaze
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { exactly_magic_project_level = { project = black_herd_project_1 level = 0 } }
				country_event = { id = black_herd_events.11 } #Lighting The Path
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened } }
			if = { 
				limit = {
					check_variable = { black_herd_sieges_var = 2 }
					check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 94 } #~800/850 exp
					exactly_magic_project_level = { project = black_herd_project_1 level = 2 }
				}
				set_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened
				country_event = { id = black_herd_events.310 } #Shattering Stone
			}
			else_if = { 
				limit = {
					check_variable = { black_herd_causalities_var = 10000 }
					check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 92 } #~550/600 exp
					exactly_magic_project_level = { project = black_herd_project_1 level = 1 }
				}
				set_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened
				country_event = { id = black_herd_events.210 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = I55_adm_advisor_project_flag
						has_country_flag = I55_dip_advisor_project_flag
						has_country_flag = I55_mil_advisor_project_flag
					}
					check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 85 } #~300/830 exp
					exactly_magic_project_level = { project = black_herd_project_1 level = 0 }
				}
				set_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened
				country_event = { id = black_herd_events.110 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = none
	}
}

#Eighard Project
namespace = magic_project_eighard_project_1
#Handler
country_event = {
	id = magic_project_eighard_project_1.0
	title = magic_project_eighard_project_1.0.t
	desc = magic_project_eighard_project_1.0.d
	picture = PIETY_eventPicture
	hidden = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = magic_project_completed_flag }
			if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = eighard_project_1 level = 3 } }
				country_event = { id = flavour_eighard.43 } #Found You
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = eighard_project_1 level = 2 } }
				country_event = { id = flavour_eighard.38 } #Only Here and Nowhere Else
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = eighard_project_1 level = 1 } }
				country_event = { id = flavour_eighard.34 } #Waves Upon Waves
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				exactly_magic_project_level = { project = eighard_project_1 level = 2 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 25 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened }
				}
				set_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened
				country_event = { #Getting Warmer...
					id = flavour_eighard.40
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 50 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened }
				}
				set_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened
				country_event = { #And Warmer...
					id = flavour_eighard.41
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 75 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_third_event_happened }
				}
				set_country_flag = magic_project_third_event_happened
				country_event = { #Very Warm...
					id = flavour_eighard.42
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				exactly_magic_project_level = { project = eighard_project_1 level = 1 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 33 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened }
				}
				set_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened
				country_event = { #Recurrent
					id = flavour_eighard.36
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 66 }
					NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened }
				} 
				set_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened
				country_event = { #Drift
					id = flavour_eighard.37
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				exactly_magic_project_level = { project = eighard_project_1 level = 0 }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 50 }
				}
				country_event = { #As You Are But Not As You Were
					id = flavour_eighard.33 
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = "magic_project_eighard_project_1.0.a"
	}
}

		name = magic_project_cangji_project.9.a
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = { has_cinder_monastery = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { has_level_2_cinder_monastery = yes }
				remove_province_modifier = V05_cinder_monastery_2_upgraded_1
				remove_province_modifier = V05_cinder_monastery_2
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = V05_cinder_monastery_2_upgraded_2
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			else = {
				remove_province_modifier = V05_cinder_monastery_1
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = V05_cinder_monastery_1_upgraded
					duration = -1
				}
			}
			remove_province_triggered_modifier = V05_sputtering_flames_effect
		}
		custom_tooltip = tooltip_magic_project_complete
		change_variable = { magic_projects_completed = 1 }
	}
}

			set_country_flag = magic_project_third_event_happened

		}

	desc = none
	picture = none
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes	

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = magic_project_completed_flag } # Stage Finishing Event
			if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = kanolowele_volcanic_armoury level = 3 } }
				country_event = { id = landslide_infantry.1299 } # A Wonder to the World - (Final) End Event 3
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = kanolowele_volcanic_armoury level = 2 } }
				country_event = { id = landslide_infantry.1199 } # A Busy Place - End Event 2
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { at_least_magic_project_level = { project = kanolowele_volcanic_armoury level = 1 } }
				country_event = { id = landslide_infantry.1099 } # A Functioning Armory - End Event 1
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Level 1 In Progress Events 
			limit = { exactly_magic_project_level = { project = kanolowele_volcanic_armoury level = 0 } }
			if = { # 20%
				limit = { check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 20 } NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened } }
				set_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened
				country_event = { id = landslide_infantry.1020 } # Laying Foundations
			}
			else_if = { # 40%

				set_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened
				country_event = { id = landslide_infantry.1040 } # Minor Eruption
			}
			else_if = { # 60%
				limit = { check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 60 } NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_third_event_happened } }
				set_country_flag = magic_project_third_event_happened
				country_event = { id = landslide_infantry.1060 } # Earthquake Shakes Foundations
			}
			else_if = { # 80%

				set_country_flag = magic_project_fourth_event_happened
				country_event = { id = landslide_infantry.1080 } # Supply lines raided
			}
		}
		else_if = { # Level 2 In Progress Events

			if = { # 20%
				limit = { check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 20 } NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened } }

				country_event = { id = landslide_infantry.1120 } # Training new recruits
			}
			else_if = { # 40%

				set_country_flag = magic_project_second_event_happened
				country_event = { id = landslide_infantry.1140 } # Magma containment failure
			}
			else_if = { # 60%
				limit = { check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 60 } NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_third_event_happened } }
				set_country_flag = magic_project_third_event_happened
				country_event = { id = landslide_infantry.1160 } # Foreign agents attempt sabotage
			}

				set_country_flag = magic_project_fourth_event_happened
				country_event = { id = landslide_infantry.1180 } # Metal cooling in container
			}
		}

			if = { # 20%
				limit = { check_variable = { current_experience_percent = 20 } NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_project_first_event_happened } }
